4.1.33 Stam S.r.l. 
Short Name STAM Type  SME Country IT 
 
 
 
http://www.stamtech.com/ 
Partner Description 
Description of organization 
STAM is a private engineering company with a staff of more than 25 people, based in Genoa, Italy. The main mission 
of the company is to provide engineering services to industries. Since its establishment in 1997, the company has 
been specializing in design and manufacturing of innovative mechanical systems, based on conventional and non -
conventional robotics and mechatronics. 
STAM has patented several devices, like transmissions and manufacturing machinery, and is experienced in design 
and integration of system mechatronics. STAM invests a significant part of its turnover in R&D, thus providing their 
customers with most qualified and edging competencies to drive development based on availability and affordability 
of technological trends. 
STAM is a SME member of E2BA and supplier of the European Space Agency with the Technology Transfer 
Programme. STAM has also developed a significant experience in working with the funding instruments of the 
European Commission, being involved in more than 50 Projects in the last 15 years. 
The Company performs all stages of the product design cycle, from conception through validation with CAD and 
FEA tools, to component and subsystem design and specification, down to the definition of tools, and production 
cycles. STAM has been deeply involved in automation, robotics and new product development in several industrial 
fields. 
Today STAM is a successful high -tech company offering engineering services and products in a number of market 
sectors including: Space, Automation & Robotics, Security & Transport and Energy. 
STAM has the ISO 9001:2008 certification for quality management systems, proving the commitment of the 
company to provide products that meet customer, applicable statutory and regulatory requirements,  through the 
effective application of the system, including processes for continual improvement and assurance of conformity to 
requirements. 
Role in the Project 
STAM is an engineering company applying engineering solutions to industrial scale. They will design and construct 
the entire monitoring and control systems of the pilot lines. STAM will provide key personnel with strong expertise 
in the respective research and development areas. These key people have participated in several international and 
national collaborative projects and will be supported by technical and administrative staff people, in order to perform 
all the project activities.  In WP2, STAM will lead activities in Task 2.1, being responsible for the upgrade of the 
pilot lines in terms of monitoring and control of the manufacturing processes to improve and optimize the quality of 
the products. STAM has collected great expertise in this role in ongoing H2020 projects such as LightCoce and 
LightMe and closed project involving pilot line optimizations and monitoring such as NANOLEAP. In WP4 STAM 
will support activities related to Task 4.3: Process Validation and Predictive modeling. In the same WP, STAM will 
contribute to Task 4.4: Data Management. Additionally, STAM will lead Task Task 7.4: Im plementation of the 
additional test cases in the OITB supported by all partners of BIOMAC. Finally, STAM will also strongly contribute 
to WP8 related to exploitation activities and WP9 about Dissemination and Communication actions.

Relevant products & services: 
1. Mechatronic solutions for industrial automation: Stam designs and develops mechatronic devices for the 
automation of tasks, based on the inputs of its customers. The machines are tailored for the specific needs 
of the process and involve solutions ranging from automation systems, to industrial and special robotics. 
2. Control systems: Stam develops both the control systems of the machines designed by the company and 
the control strategies for systems developed by other parties. The design of control systems may include: 
analysis of control parameters, identification of sensors and actuators, selection of COTS parts. 
3. Control algorithms: this is the core activity in the development of a control system. Stam can perform the 
analysis and simulation of the whole process, the identification of the most suitable parameters and the 
coding of the actual laws that govern the process.

1. nanoCOOL (FP7-GA n. 314701): “An Energy Efficient Air Conditioning systems with Temperature and 
Humidity independent controls based on the combination of a Liquid Desiccants Cycle with an adapted 
conventional air cooling system” (www.nanocoolproject.eu) 
2. NANOLEAP  (H2020-GA n. 646397): “Nanocomposite for building constructions and civil

Infrastructure & technical equipment 
The offices of STAM are located in the centre of Genova, very close to several high -tech companies and to the 
University of Genova, with which Stam has been successfully collaborating for more than a decade. STAM has also 
a workshop and a laboratory to develop, test and tune prototype of mechanical and mechatronic systems. 
STAM provides engineering and management services during the overall engineering life cycle thanks to its set of 
facilities and software capabilities. In particular the main facilities are the technical software tools presented below: 
• Monitoring system development and integration 
• FEM/FEA (ANSYS): static, dynamic, harmonic, linear, non-linear, explosions (fast dynamics), composite 
materials, multi-physics. 
• CAD/CAE design (PTC Creo): solid modelling of parts and assemblies, detailed design and production of 
executive drawings, CAM interface, optimization. 
• Agent-based modelling (AnyLogic): models for simulating actions and interactions of autonomous agents 
(individual or collective entities) to assess their effects on the system. 
• Numerical simulations (Matlab & Simulink): numerical modelling and simulation of complex systems and 
control.

UniSMART is the Foundation of the University of Padova, top ranked Italian University, in charge of managing 
all the technology transfer and innovation consulting activities directed to companies, industrial associations, 
professionals, investors, banks, and other public and private bodies – both on a national and interna tional scale. 
UniSMART systematically assists its 5000 researchers from 32 Departments as well as its 60,000 students in 
maximizing the exposure of their research and talents, making sure it is brought in front of the most relevant 
stakeholders to generate impact on society. This include idea contests and hackathons as well as contamination 
labs to name a few. UniSMART daily collaborates with industry and public stakeholders by: 
- working closely together with entrepreneurs, c-level execs and public officers to investigate their most pressing 
innovation challenges and to support them elaborating effective strategies protecting each side’s IP; 
- identifying the best-matching set of technologies, multidisciplinary skills and competences in the university that 
can be used to solve innovation challenges; 
- managing complex research projects, ensuring on-time and on-quality delivery while guaranteeing full protection 
and the best valorisation of all intellectual property; 
- organization of life-long learning activities, seminars, dissemination events, administration of University’s master 
courses. 
UniSMART possesses valuable know-how and expertise in the European research and innovation landscape. It 
has supported several R&D teams, technological ventures, s tart-ups and SMEs as well as large private or public 
organizations to the commercialization of their research and innovation outcomes. The IP management is part of 
the core business for two main reasons: each collaborative project requires special care for  both University’s and 
other partner’s sensible data; UniSMART is the sole authorized agent when speaking about negotiation of 
University’s patent licensing. 
 
Activities within the project 
Knowledge Management and IP. UniSMART will assist UNIPD in the orga nisation of knowledge management 
seminars and in analising the Freedom to Operate for the technologies and inventions produced during the project 
(WP8). (7 months + 10,000 for Knowledge seminars). 
 
Key staff involved in the project

managing Director of UniSMART he has worked in the education sector managing both education activities, such

complement their vision and ideas designing scalable commercial strategies, supporting the creat ion of “ad hoc” 
education offerings and opportunities. He has implemented education and seminar activities both in presence and 
on line, taking advantage of the strongest and safer tools available.

ACCIONA Construcción has a collaboration framework agreement with the Fundación 
Agustín de Betancourt (FAB), setting a stable and permanent cooperation in scientific and 
technological issues for the support at the i mplementation and execution of national and 
international R&D projects at which ACCIONA Construcción participates. 
 
In the context of this collaboration agreement, FAB makes available to ACCIONA 
seconded researchers, on a project-by-project basis, to support the technical and scientific 
execution of the works to be carried out in ACCIONA’s R&D projects, which work in 
ACCIONA premises under its direct supervision. 
 
Fundación Agustín de Betancourt is  a cultural Foundation with pri vate and pe rmanent 
character, Spanish nationality, non-profit and public interest, with legal personality and 
full legal capacity to act. It was created in 1977 in the Polytechnic University of Madrid 
(UPM) under the impulse of four engineers interested in promoting research, innovation, 
technology transfer and collaboration between universities and industry. 
 
Since its constitution and in accordance with its statutory objectives, the Foundation has 
cooperated with the University in fulfilling its foundational objectives: promote and develop 
fundamental and applied research, technological development and innovation.
